 flipcart ke mukhya vittiya adhikari kalyaan krishnamurthi ne kaha, "asus ko ham bharat ko dhyaan main rakhkar smartphone banane ke liye apane data aadhaarit anusandhan or takneekee kaushal muhaiyaa karaayenge
 "comments asus ne bhi apane digital siesaar (korporate saamaajik bhagidaari) ke tahat jaruratmandon ko digital sakshartaa muhaiyaa karaane kii ghoshnaa kii he
 ASUS CEO Jerry Shen said, "we see a lot of opportunity in building products and services that meet India's specific market needs
" flipcart ke saath bhagidaari se hamaara lakshya bhartiya upabhoktaaon kii jaruraton ke bare main adhik jaankaree hasil karnaa he, jo hamen bhartiya bazaar ke liye or bhi upyukt utpaadon kaa vikaas karne main madad kar saktaa he
 " company ne ek bayaan main kaha ki is bhagidaari ke tahat 23 april ko 'jenphone maiks pro' laanch kiya jayega
 Kalyan Krishnamurthy, Chief Financial Officer, Flipkart, said, "asus we will provide our data-based research and technical skills to make smartphones in keeping with India
 "tippaniyan ASUS has also announced to provide digital literacy to the needy under its digital CSR (corporate Social Partnership)
 asus ke mukhya kaaryakari adhikari jeri shen ne kaha, "ham bharat kii vishesh bazaar kii jaruraton ko puraa karanevaale utpaadon or sevaaon ke nirmaan main kaaphi avasar dekhte hai
 Our goal in partnership with Flipkart is to gain more knowledge about the needs of Indian consumers, which can help us to develop more suitable products for the Indian market
